FNV VOLUMETRIC LOCAL-SHADOW BIND AND LIFETIME CONTRACT AUDIT

Proven starting point:
1. A selected 0x250-byte local-shadow object retains a type-0x2B rendered texture at +0x10C.
2. Type 0x2B is normally D24X8 but changes to A8R8G8B8 in the ATI compatibility path.
3. SimpleShadow packages and a separate draw-scoped ShadowProj matrix are registered by PPLighting.
4. Earlier audits did not prove that the selected object's +0x10C texture reaches that package.
5. The first value-copy audit proved that RenderShadowMaps sees a capped shadow-selected subset, not all active lights.

Closure questions:
1. Which object owns the PPLighting +0x60 list, and when is its shadow plus non-shadow membership stable?
2. Does that list include player, muzzle, projectile, scripted, point, and spot lights once per world frame?
3. Can its ShadowSceneLight values be copied once without retaining its +0xF8 native light pointer?
4. Which live draw path dispatches SimpleShadow vertex 89-91 and pixel 152-157?
5. How does the same selected light's +0x10C texture reach a texture stage, and which stage is it?
6. What sampler, comparison, bias, channel, and ATI encoding rules decode that texture?
7. Which projection matrix is paired with that exact texture, and where is the pairing established?
8. Can a hook retain both resources with explicit references until OMV finishes its atmosphere draw?
9. At what render phase are production complete, filtering complete, and pool invalidation impossible?
10. Does NVR replace any list, producer, package, format, or lifetime owner in this chain?

Required result:
Either a complete copied texture-plus-matrix ABI with explicit lifetime rules, or proof that OMV must own local shadow resources.
